<p>The <b>2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</b> was the 15th edition of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="UEFA European Under-19 Championship">UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a> (65th edition if the Under-18 and Junior eras are included), the annual European international youth <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> championship contested by the men's under-19 national teams of <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> member associations. <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, which were selected by UEFA on 20 March 2012, hosted the tournament between 11 and 24 July 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-host_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-host-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>A total of eight teams competed in the final tournament, with players born on or after 1 January 1997 eligible to participate.</p>
<p>Same as previous editions held in even-numbered years, the tournament acted as the UEFA qualifiers for the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="FIFA U-20 World Cup">FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>. The top five teams qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a> in South Korea as the UEFA representatives. This was decreased from the previous six teams, as FIFA decided to give one of the slots originally reserved for UEFA to the <a href="/wiki/Oceania_Football_Confederation" title="Oceania Football Confederation">Oceania Football Confederation</a> starting from 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualification">Qualification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Qualification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship_qualification" title="2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship qualification">2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship qualification</a></div>
<p>The national teams from all 54 UEFA member associations entered the competition. With Germany automatically qualified as hosts, the other 53 teams contested a qualifying competition to determine the remaining seven spots in the final tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> The qualifying competition consisted of two rounds: the qualifying round, which took place in autumn 2015, and the elite round, which took place in spring 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-5">[5]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_draw">Final draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Final draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The final draw was held on 12 April 2016, 18:00 <a href="/wiki/Central_European_Summer_Time" title="Central European Summer Time">CEST</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B02:00" title="UTC+02:00">UTC+2</a>), at the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_Arena_(Stuttgart)" title="Mercedes-Benz Arena (Stuttgart)">Mercedes-Benz Arena</a> in <a href="/wiki/Stuttgart" title="Stuttgart">Stuttgart</a>, Germany.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> The eight teams were drawn into two groups of four teams. There was no seeding, except that hosts Germany were assigned to position A1 in the draw.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Venues">Venues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Venues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Squads">Squads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Squads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship_squads" title="2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship squads">2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship squads</a></div>
<p>Each national team had to submit a squad of 18 players.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Match_officials">Match officials</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Match officials">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A total of 6 referees, 8 assistant referees and 2 fourth officials were appointed for the final tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></p>
<div>
<table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">

</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan"><img alt="Azerbaijan" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1200" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg/46px-Flag_of_Azerbaijan.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Aliyar_Aghayev" title="Aliyar Aghayev">Aliyar Aghayev</a> (<a href="/wiki/Association_of_Football_Federations_of_Azerbaijan" title="Association of Football Federations of Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>)</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain"><img alt="Spain" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Alejandro José Hernández Hernández (<a href="/wiki/Royal_Spanish_Football_Federation" title="Royal Spanish Football Federation">Spain</a>)</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania"><img alt="Romania" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="600" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/23px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/35px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/45px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Radu Marian Petrescu (<a href="/wiki/Romanian_Football_Federation" title="Romanian Football Federation">Romania</a>)</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_stage">Group stage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Group stage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="457" data-file-width="610" height="375" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg/500px-2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg/750px-2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg/1000px-2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg.png 2x" width="500"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2016_UEFA_U-19_European_Championship_map.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Results of teams participating in 2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The final tournament schedule was confirmed on 18 April 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></p>
<p>The group winners and runners-up advanced to the semi-finals and qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>. The third-placed teams entered the FIFA U-20 World Cup play-off. <span id="Tiebreakers"></span></p>
<dl>
<dt>Tiebreakers</dt>
</dl>
<p>The teams were ranked according to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Points_(association_football)" title="Points (association football)">points</a> (3 points for a win, 1 point for a draw, 0 points for a loss). If two or more teams were equal on points on completion of the group matches, the following tie-breaking criteria were applied, in the order given, to determine the rankings:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_5-2"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>Higher number of points obtained in the group matches played among the teams in question;</li>
<li>Superior <a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">goal difference</a> resulting from the group matches played among the teams in question;</li>
<li>Higher number of goals scored in the group matches played among the teams in question;</li>
<li>If, after having applied criteria 1 to 3, teams still had an equal ranking, criteria 1 to 3 were reapplied exclusively to the group matches between the teams in question to determine their final rankings. If this procedure did not lead to a decision, criteria 5 to 9 applied;</li>
<li>Superior goal difference in all group matches;</li>
<li>Higher number of goals scored in all group matches;</li>
<li>If only two teams had the same number of points, and they were tied according to criteria 1 to 6 after having met in the last round of the group stage, their rankings were determined by a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shoot-out</a> (not used if more than two teams had the same number of points, or if their rankings were not relevant for qualification for the next stage).</li>
<li>Lower disciplinary points total based only on yellow and red cards received in the group matches (red card = 3 points, yellow card = 1 point, expulsion for two yellow cards in one match = 3 points);</li>
<li>Drawing of lots.</li>
</ol>
<p>All times were local, <a href="/wiki/Central_European_Summer_Time" title="Central European Summer Time">CEST</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B02:00" title="UTC+02:00">UTC+2</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Knockout_stage">Knockout stage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Knockout stage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the knockout stage, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra_time_(association_football)" title="Extra time (association football)">extra time</a> and <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shoot-out</a> were used to decide the winner if necessary.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_5-3"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 2 May 2016, the UEFA Executive Committee agreed that the competition would be part of the <a href="/wiki/International_Football_Association_Board" title="International Football Association Board">International Football Association Board</a>'s trial to allow a <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">fourth substitute</a> to be made during extra time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> In the FIFA U-20 World Cup play-off, <a href="/wiki/Michel_Vlap" title="Michel Vlap">Michel Vlap</a> of the Netherlands became the first ever fourth substitute, replacing <a href="/wiki/Laros_Duarte" title="Laros Duarte">Laros Duarte</a> at half-time in extra time, followed later by <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Iyoha" title="Emmanuel Iyoha">Emmanuel Iyoha</a> of Germany replacing <a href="/wiki/Jannes_Horn" title="Jannes Horn">Jannes Horn</a> in the 110th minute.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="FIFA_U-20_World_Cup_play-off">FIFA U-20 World Cup play-off</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: FIFA U-20 World Cup play-off">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Winner qualified for <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualified_teams_for_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup">Qualified teams for FIFA U-20 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Qualified teams for FIFA U-20 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following five teams from UEFA qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2017 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable sortable" style="text-align: left;">
<tr>
<th>Team</th>
<th>Qualified on</th>
<th>Previous appearances in tournament<sup><b><a href="#1">1</a></b></sup></th>
